\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Instead\ of\ directly\ including\ vulkan.h,\ we\ include\ platform-\/specific\ parts\ of\ the\ SDK\ manually}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ is\ necessary\ to\ avoid\ including\ platform\ headers\ in\ some\ cases\ (which\ vulkan.h\ does\ unconditionally)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ replace\ them\ with\ forward\ declarations,\ which\ makes\ build\ times\ faster\ and\ avoids\ macro\ conflicts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Note\ that\ we\ only\ replace\ platform-\/specific\ headers\ when\ the\ headers\ are\ known\ to\ be\ problematic:\ very\ large}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ or\ slow\ to\ compile\ (Windows),\ or\ introducing\ unprefixed\ macros\ which\ can\ cause\ conflicts\ (Windows,\ Xlib).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
